<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> persoon enkelvoud tegenwoordige <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a><br />

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>Ga</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a>?</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a>!</i> </li>
<li><i>Tijdens <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> geest <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrije</a> teugel <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> verkeerd <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> pauze <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> hersens <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> arbeidsobjecten <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> doormalen. ***gaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a> (64)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gâen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gān</i>, from a fusion of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gāną</i> and <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ganganą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰeh₁-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰengʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go, to move from one place to another
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> strand.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm <b>going</b> to the beach.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> nergens naartoe.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That car isn't <b>going</b> anywhere.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave or depart, to move away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>Morgen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They're <b>leaving</b> again tomorrow.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lead (in a direction)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> Limburg.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This road <b>goes</b> all the way to Limburg.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to proceed (well or poorly)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <b>went</b> well.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">How <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> it <b>going</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That won't <b>work</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Forms the future tense of a verb, similarly to English going to future tense</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not going</b> to work anyway.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start to, begin to, to be going to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> zon <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> schijnen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The sun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>starting to</b> shine again.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:slapen.html>slapen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm <b>going</b> to sleep.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> regenen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It's <b>going to</b> start raining soon.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zullen.html>zullen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also used for the future tense, but sounds more formal</li>
<li>In questions, the past tense <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a>(<a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>)</i> in the sense of “to go” can be used to indicate the present. In Dutch, one can ask “Ging <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> verjaardag <a href = vnd.unilang:vanavond.html>vanavond</a>?” which means “<b>Are</b> you still <b>going</b> to that birthday party tonight?”. The question implies there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a plan to go to the said party, and asks for confirmation that the plan <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still on. This exceptional use of the past tense with a present meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also seen for the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></i>.</li></ul>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">gang</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i>Werkwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">ergatief</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> bepaalde richting bewegen, meestal <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> spreker <a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> Amerika.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li>mogelijk <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geburen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">geburien</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to happen, occur</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gaburjaną</i>. <dl><dd><ul><li><i>Piet <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gebruiken.html>gebruikte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> ladder <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> dak <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> (43)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">negeen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ne <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>gene</a></i>, (also as <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">engheen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">chein</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ghein</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">nehein</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not one; none</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kein</i>.
</p>

<li>none</li></ol>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>This word, when used at all, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually preceded by a definite article or a demonstrative. Because of this, the uninflected form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very rare.

***gek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gek.html>gek</a> (219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geck</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">madman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Earlier origin unknown, possibly dialectal and/or from unknown substrate; however, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Geck</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Jeck</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">geek</i> (see etymology there).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gek.html>gek</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gek.html>gekker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gekst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crazy, mad
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maakt.html>maakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gek.html>gek</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>You make <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> crazy.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>ludicrous, farcical</li>
<li>silly, playful</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a> (158)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gheld</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ghelt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*geldą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reward, gift, money</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰeldʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">yield</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>Geld</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">money</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">jild</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">gjald</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">payment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌲𐌹𐌻𐌳</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gild</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tribute</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***geloof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloof</a> (281)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>gelove</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gelôve</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gilōvo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*galaubô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>geloven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloofje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>belief, conviction.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> faith, religion.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The genitive form of the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i>des geloofs</i>. Of its alternative form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>gelove</a></i> it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i>des <a href = vnd.unilang:geloven.html>geloven</a></i> or <i>des geloves</i>. In Dutch, the genitive <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not commonly used outside of fixed expressions and literary language, but can be frequently encountered in early modern Dutch texts.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">belief<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> conviction</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">overtuiging</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">godsdienst</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">religie</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bijgeloof</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span></li>

***gelukkig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a> (466)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geluckig</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">geluk</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gelukkigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>happy</li>
<li>pleased, satisfied</li>
<li>lucky</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkige</a> verjaardag</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>Gelukkig</a> Nieuwjaar</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Indefinite adjectives describing people often remain uninflected, if they express a personal quality. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not stylistically neutral, but has a formal, rhetorical or poetic ring to it, and can occasionally distinguish literal meanings of an adjective from a more figurative one. Furthermore, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only done with some nouns, not all. Hence, besides the regularly inflected "<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>", the uninflected "<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>" can also be encountered.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>luckily</li>
<li>thankfully</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i>Bijvoeglijk naamwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li>in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> tevredene toestand <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> voelen
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>"<a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>Veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> vergissen <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:maakt.html>maakt</a>" <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd>

***geweldig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geweldig.html>geweldig</a> (282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geweldich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*giweldig</i>, composed of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">giwald</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">-ig</i>. The base word descends from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gawaldiz</i>. Synchronically equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">geweld</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geweldig.html>geweldig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geweldig.html>geweldiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">geweldigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tremendous, great</li>
<li>awesome, wonderful</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i>Bijvoeglijk naamwoord</i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a> (212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">got</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gudą</i>, from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰutós</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">invoked (one)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gott</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">gud</i>.
</p>

***goed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> (49)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">goet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">guot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gōdaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰedʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beter.html>beter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">good</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voel.html>voel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I feel <b>good</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a></b> informatiebron.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>good</b> source of information.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">correct</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">right</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">factually or morally</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Helaas, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> antwoord <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Unfortunately, that answer <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not <b>correct</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Sommige <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> verschil <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> fout.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Some people can't see the difference between <b>right</b> and wrong.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">fout</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">verkeerd</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">all right</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fine</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That's <b>all right</b>. That's <b>fine</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<p>Next to the regular form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a></i>, the form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">goeie</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also used informally.
</p>

<ol><li>well
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>speelt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></b> tennis.</i> — He plays tennis well.</dd>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Adverbs are the same as adjectives, so also the archaic adverb <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> (<i>well</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now <i><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i>, though it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still used in compounds, see <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.vandale.nl/vandale/opzoeken/woordenboek/?zoekwoord=wel">words starting with "<a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a>" in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> Dale</i></a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goederen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goedje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> goods

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clothes, clothing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>Voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> sollicitatiegesprek <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> zondagse <b><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></b> gestoken, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> desondanks sjofel <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> donned his <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> <b>clothes</b> for the job interview, but nevertheless made a shabby impression.</span></div></dd>

***haar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> (56)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hiro</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hezōi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">personal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Third-person singular, feminine object pronoun: her
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeg.html>zeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></b> (1), <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunt.html>kunt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></b> (2) <a href = vnd.unilang:beter.html>beter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> mailtje sturen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I’ll mention it to <b>her</b>, but you’d better send <b>her</b> a mail as well.</span></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>(1) accusative personal pronoun, (2) dative personal pronoun</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hira</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hezōz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></strong> (<i>dependent possessive, independent possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>hare</a></b>, <i>contracted form</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">'r</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Third-person singular, feminine possessive adjective: her
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:" class="extiw" title="w:nl:">Wikipedia</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Dood_van_Diana_Frances_Spencer" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Dood van Diana Frances Spencer"><a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>Dood</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Diana Frances Spencer</a></i>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>Op</a> 31 augustus 1997 overleed Diana Frances Spencer, Prinses <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Wales <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> auto-ongeluk in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> tunnel <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Pont <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> l'Alma in Parijs, <a href = vnd.unilang:samen.html>samen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a> Dodi Al-Fayed <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> chauffeur.</i>  |  On August 31, 1997, Diana Frances Spencer, Princess of Wales, died in a car accident in a tunnel by the Pont <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> l'Alma in Paris, together with her friend Dodi Al-Fayed and their driver.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">heur</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">archaic or dialectal variant</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_2">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hiro</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hezǫ̂</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_3">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></strong> (<i>dependent possessive, independent possive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>hare</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Third-person plural possessive adjective: their</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>Haar</a></i> (“their”) <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the normal Middle Dutch form for all genders in the plural. In modern Dutch, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> successively replaced <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> in this function. Some writers of the 19th and early 20th century made a learned distinction, using <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> as the masculine and neuter plural, but <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> for the feminine in both singular and plural: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>hunne</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwen.html>vrouwen</a></i> (“men and their wives”) versus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwen.html>vrouwen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>hare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a></i> (“women and their husbands”).</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">their</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4_2">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hâer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hār</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hērą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">haren</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">haartje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hair</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">collection of hairs</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hair</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">mammalian keratin filament</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The noun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> traditionally neuter in all senses. As a countable noun, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now sometimes of common gender.</li></ul>

***hart.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hart</a> (483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">herte</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">harte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">herta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hertô</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱḗr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hart</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>harten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>heart, main muscle pumping blood through the body:</li>
<li>The center point or zone of an object, image etc.</li>
<li>The core or essence of some thing, reasoning etc.</li>
<li>Compassionate or similar feelings</li></ol>

***hebben.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> (50)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*habjaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*keh₂p-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have, to possess, own, hold
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>Hebt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> minuut?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you <b>have</b> a minute?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bezitten</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be afflicted with a disease
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a></b> longkanker.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>have</b> lung cancer.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form the perfect tense of the active voice of most verbs, together with a past participle.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> koekje opgegeten.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>have</b> eaten the biscuit.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> gewassen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <b><a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a></b> only just washed their car.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b>has</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> to walk home.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>have</b> heard him speak.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You should <b>have</b> done that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> must, to be obliged to, to be to</li></ol>

***heel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> (130)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hêel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hēl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hailaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">heelst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>complete, full, whole</li>
<li>unbroken, undamaged, untarnished</li>
<li>big, enormous, significant</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_3">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">gans</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">volledig</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">geheel</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">helen</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">heil</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>very</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Although an adverb, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></i> may be inflected as well (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a></i>) to match the following adjective, by analogy with the inflection of adjectives in Dutch.
</p><p>. For example, both of these sentences are correct:
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>very</b> large tree.</span></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>very</b> large tree.</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<p>The latter form may be regarded as informal and less appropriate for formal writing.
</p>

***heen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a> (280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">henen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">away from here, hence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>away
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> baron <a href = vnd.unilang:gaf.html>gaf</a> den koetsier <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> wenk <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> rijtuig rolde <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The baron <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>gave</a> the coachman a sign and the carriage rolled <b>away</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">postpositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to, towards
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>Waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a></b>?</i>
<dl><dd>Where am I going?</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gone, outside the boundaries of the norms
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> ver <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> already too far <b>gone</b>. (could imply being drunk or having lost his mind)</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a> (197)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></i>, by analogy with the inflection of adjectives that follow.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></i></span></span>
<ul><li><b>2018</b> 25 June, Carolien Roelants, “Goed <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuws.html>nieuws</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> Jemen plus <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> Hollandse kortzichtigheid”, nrc.nl:
<dl><dd><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>Hele</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a></b> dure koffie, <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> name bestemd <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Aziatische markt, want Europa <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> „gevoeliger <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> prijs”, <a href = vnd.unilang:zegt.html>zegt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> elegant.
<dl><dd>Very good, very expensive coffee, especially destined for the Asiatic market, for “Europe <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more sensitive to the price”, he says elegantly.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">henne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*henna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanjō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*keh₂n-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">hennen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">hennetje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">haan</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></a>, female chicken; female of a related species.</li>
<li>A female of the species of birds brooding on the ground.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> 'bird', colloquial term for a human female</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>(female chicken) <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kip</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kieken</span></li>
<li>(brooding bird) <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kloek</span></li>
<li>(female human; informal) <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kippetje</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">duifje</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i>Zelfstandig naamwoord</i></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Persoonlijk_voornaamwoord"><i>Persoonlijk voornaamwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li>persoonlijk voornaamwoord <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> derde persoon meervoud in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> functie <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> lijdend voorwerp <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> voorzetsels. Voornamelijk <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruiken.html>gebruikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> verwijzen <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> personen, <a href = vnd.unilang:soms.html>soms</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> dieren.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> vergaderingsruimte.</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>Met</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> conferentie.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***het.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> (4)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> contracted to <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">'t</i> in usual speech. This form <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> interpreted as being the same as the neuter pronoun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> (etymology 2, see below), which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> contracted in the same way. This then led to the modern form/spelling <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i>, which some might see as being unetymological.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Article">Article</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>the <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the neuter definite article</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> boek</i>
<dl><dd><b>the</b> book</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a></i>
<dl><dd><b>the</b> girl</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hetzelfde.html>hetzelfde</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hit</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">it</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hit</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*it</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>it; <span class="use-with-mention">third-person singular, neuter, subjective</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mooi.html>mooi</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beetje.html>beetje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>klein</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>It</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a nice house, but a little small.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>it; <span class="use-with-mention">third-person singular, neuter, objective</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>Kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>?</i>
<dl><dd>Can you see <b>it</b> well?</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>doe</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I'll do <b>it</b> if you want <b>it</b>. (i.e. "if you want <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to")</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> honger, <a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>geef</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> boterham.</i>
<dl><dd>The girl <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> hungry, give her a sandwich.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>it; <span class="use-with-mention">impersonal</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>It</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> late.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a></b> regent alweer.</i>
<dl><dd><b>It'</b>s raining again.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b>?</i>
<dl><dd>How <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>it</b> going?</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>This pronoun can combine with a preposition to form a pronominal adverb. When this occurs, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> changed into its adverbial/locative counterpart <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></i>. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.</li>
<li>In a double-object construction with another pronoun, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally the direct object but precedes the other pronoun: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a>!</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Give it back to him!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare regional English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Give it him back!</i>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> different from other neuter pronouns, which usually follow the indirect object: <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a>!</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Give that back to him!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Persoonlijk_voornaamwoord"><i>Persoonlijk voornaamwoord</i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>3e persoon enkelvoud onzijdig.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> (32)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hē₂r</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>here</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with a preposition</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> this</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>With a preposition, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used instead of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></i> to create a pronominal adverb. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>Hier</a>!</b> (</i>uitroep, <a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>kom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plek.html>plek</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> hond of <a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>klein</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a><i>)</i> </li>

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> locatief deel <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> voornaamwoordelijk bijwoord. <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> vervangt <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> aanwijzend voornaamwoord (nabij) <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a></b> </i>(<a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></b>)<i> </i> </li></ul></dd>
<dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i>`<b><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>Hier</a></b> links <a href = vnd.unilang:vindt.html>vindt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a>  bibliotheek;  <a href = vnd.unilang:zei.html>zei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> gids, '<a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achter.html>daarachter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> groene zaal <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Chinese <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-Grand_Hotel_Europa,_p._15_2-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Grand_Hotel_Europa,_p._15-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></dd></dl></li></ol>

***hij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> (15)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hē</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><i>Third-person singular, masculine, subjective:</i> he.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>loopt</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>He</b> walks.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>When the word occurs other than as the first word of a clause and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not emphatically stressed, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually pronounced as <span class="IPA">/i/</span>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a completely accepted pronunciation in standard speech.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> (52)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">huo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>(<i>forms a the parallel comparative</i>) the ... the

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Second <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a></i> can be replaced by <i>des <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i>; there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no difference between the two as they are purely a matter of preference, both are commonly used throughout the Dutch-speaking regions.
</p>
