***hoi.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>hoi</a> (515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly a spontaneous alteration of the interjection <i>ho</i>. The use as a joyful exclamation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> attested from the 16th century; use as an informal greeting appears only in the 20th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>hoi</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A greeting acknowledging someone’s arrival or presence, comparable to English hey, hi
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>Hoi</a>,</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a>?</i> — Hey, how's it going?</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An exclamation of joy.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> tante in Marokko <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a>, hiep <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>hoi</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I have an aunt in Morocco and she's coming <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, yippee <b>yay</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoihoi</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hallo.html>hallo</a></span></li>

***hoofd.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a> (372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hôvet</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hôoft</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hōvit</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haubudą</i>. The sense “oral sex” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantic_loan" class="extiw" title="w:Semantic loan">semantic loan</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">head</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofdje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>head</li>
<li>head (of an organisation), chief, boss</li>
<li>a breakwater, jetty or pier at the entrance of a sea harbour</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncommon<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> oral sex</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoofd-</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoofddeksel</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoofddoek</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoofdpijn</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">doodshoofd</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">havenhoofd</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">opperhoofd</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">staatshoofd</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">voorhoofd</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i>Zelfstandig naamwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>

***hoop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a> (297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hope</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hopa</i>, from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hopon</i> (modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hopen</a></i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hope</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>A hope, aspiration, wish</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_4">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hopeloos</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a> (228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">modal particle indicating reassurance or confidence from the speaker:</span> certainly, surely, at all, <span class="use-with-mention">but often weak and untranslatable</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:straks.html>Straks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a>! — <a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genoeg.html>genoeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'ll be late! — Nah, <b>surely</b> not, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> have plenty of time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>Wilt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> bonnetje? — <a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bedankt.html>bedankt</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you want the receipt? — No, thanks.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">modal particle indicating disagreement or a certain nuance with an earlier statement:</span> regardless, despite that, anyway, you know
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> kou <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>valt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a>. — <a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>Nou</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vind.html>vind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> koud <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The cold isn't so bad. — Well, I still think it's pretty cold <b>regardless</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a> (304)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hōren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*hauʀijan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hauzijaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂ḱh₂owsyéti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hear

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be supposed to, to be meant to

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be appropriate, polite or agreeing with social norms (lit. to be heard of)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a> (232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">haldan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haldaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a particular state</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> tanden <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> schoon <b><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You should <b>keep</b> your teeth properly clean.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hou.html>Hou</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:handen.html>handen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Keep</b> your hands off!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of animals</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep, to care for

<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(clarification of this definition <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> needed)</span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hold
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> gesprek <b><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></b></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">to <b>hold</b> a conversation</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

***huis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> (155)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">huus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hūs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hūsą</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">osso</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>house
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">osso</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Case forms of this noun remain in, albeit very limited, use:
</p>
<ul><li>The definite genitive <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">des huizes</i> to mean “of the family, household”, e.g. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> dame des huizes</i> (“the lady of the house”), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a> des huizes</i> (“a friend of the family”).</li>
<li>The dative <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">huize</i> in prepositional expressions used chiefly referring to large manors or jokingly, e.g. <i>in huize Mulder</i> (“at the Mulders’ house”). It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also used in a formal manner in the fixed expression <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ten huize <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">at the house of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hulpe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hulpa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hulpiz</i>.

***hun.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> (164)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></strong> (<i>personal</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>The dative case of the third-person plural personal pronoun:</i> them, to them.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">proscribed</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>The accusative case of the third-person plural personal pronoun:</i> them.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The difference between <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></i> (as direct object) and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> (as indirect object) does not stem from actual language usage, but <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> created artificially by the prescriptive grammarian Christiaen <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Heule in the 17th century in an attempt to differentiate between the accusative (direct object) and dative case (indirect object), a distinction that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> then commonly made in the definite article and certain pronouns, but not the personal pronouns.
</p><p>In practice, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> have been used interchangeably in Modern Dutch since the language has lost its grammatical case system. Many native speakers are not aware or have trouble remembering when to use the one or the other, in part because of the rule's artificiality, in part because the distinction in form between the accusative and dative case has not been preserved anywhere else in the language. As a consequence, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> common to hear sentences where they are used in the exactly opposite way from <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Heule's rule; for example:
</p>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></b> verraden.</i> (“He has betrayed <b>them</b>.”)</li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></b> uitgegaan.</i> (“They have gone out with them.”)</li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>gegeven</a>.</i> (“I have given it to them.”)</li></ul>
<p>When the pronoun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unstressed, the problem can be circumvented by using the reduced form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i>:
</p>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b> verraden.</i></li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b> uitgegaan.</i></li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>gegeven</a>.</i></li></ul>
<p>For more information, see <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Hen_of_hun" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Hen of hun">the article in the Dutch Wikipedia</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_3">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></strong> (<i>personal</i>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dependent possessive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>independent possessive</i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>hunne</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>The third-person plural possessive pronoun:</i> their.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_2">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="NavFrame" style="float: left; width: 65em">
<div class="NavHead" style="background: CCCCFF;">Dutch personal pronouns</div>
<div class="NavContent">

</div></div>
<p><br clear="all" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely a replacement of or based on dialectal Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hullie</i> or a variant thereof, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a contraction of <i><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hunlieden</span></i> or <i><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hunlui</span></i>, a compound of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> ("them") + <i>lieden</i> or <i>lui</i> (both meaning "men, people"), which then translates roughly into "them-people". Possibly reinfluenced by or confused with the possessive <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i>. This etymology explains why usage of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> occurs only when referring to people, never to objects. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afrikaans" class="extiw" title="w:Afrikaans">Afrikaans</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="af">hulle</i>, which also stems from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hunlui</i>, but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now used also for things. For more information, see <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Hun_als_onderwerp" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Hun als onderwerp">the article in the Dutch Wikipedia</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_4">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></strong> (<i>personal</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">proscribed<span class="ib-comma">,</span> regiolectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>The nominative case of the third-person plural personal pronoun:</i> they (only referring to people).</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The use of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></i> as a subject <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> considered incorrect or substandard by most speakers, both in written and spoken language, and only occurs in the Netherlands.</li></ul>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Persoonlijk_voornaamwoord"><i>Persoonlijk voornaamwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li>persoonlijk voornaamwoord derde persoon meervoud, datief, specifiek verwijzend <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> groep personen
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>gegeven</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>idee</a> (238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>idee</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>idee</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>idee</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">idea</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a (Platonic) idea; archetype</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἰδέα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idéa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">notion, pattern</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εἴδω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eídō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I see</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">idée</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>idee</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>ideeën</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">philosophy</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> idea, notion</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> normally considered to be a neuter noun (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>idee</a></i>), but it can be considered feminine (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>idee</a></i>) for a philosophical or abstract idea.
</p>

***ie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a> (257)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely from earlier <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hi</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>Third-person singular, masculine, subjective, mute form:</i> he.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">How does <b>he</b> do that?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely from unstressed <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Holland" class="extiw" title="w:Holland">Holland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>Second-person singular, mute form:</i> you.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>Heb</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> krant <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> gelezen?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Have <b>you</b> already read the newspaper?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">io</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ie.html>ie</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> always, every time, continuously</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ever, sometime, at some point</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> entirely replaced by words like <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a></i> ("always, every time") and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ooit.html>ooit</a></i> ("ever, sometime, at some point") by the late 16th century.
</p>

***iedereen.html

***iemand.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> (111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ieman</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">iemant</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ieman</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ioman</i>. A compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">io</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">always, ever</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiw</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mann-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***iets.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> (75)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">iet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">iewet</i>, a contraction of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">iowiht</i>.
The Middle Dutch word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> formed out of the articles <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ie-</i> meaning 'anything', and a second article corresponding with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wicht</i>, 'creature', of which its original meaning likely has been 'thing'. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Limburgish" class="extiw" title="w:Limburgish">Limburgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="li">get</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Franconian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Central Franconian language">Central Franconian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-cfr">jet</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">aught</i>.
</p><p>In the word, the suffix -s has been shaped under influence of the older <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a></i> wherein -s <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the ending of an old partitive genitive.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>something
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>Mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>?</i> : May it be something more?</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>Mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> minder <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>?</i> : May it be something less?</dd></dl></li>
<li>anything
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:anders.html>Anders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a>?</i> : Anything else? (literally: Otherwise yet/still something?)</dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ic</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ek</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*éǵh₂</i>. </p>
<ol><li>duidt bevestiging, instemming, toestemming, inwilliging of toegeving <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a>

***jaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> (163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jâer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">jār</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jērą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yeh₁-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>year</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The singular form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> normally in used after numerals and stock phrases instead of plurals but both are considered correct grammatically. Thus, it would be more common to say "<i><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>vele</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaren</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geleden.html>geleden</a></i>" – many years ago; but "<i><a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geleden.html>geleden</a></i>" – "three years ago" or in "<i>in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>laatste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a></b></i>" as opposed to "<i>in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>laatste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaren</a></i>" ("in the last couple of years").
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_3">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***jij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> (33)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ji</i>, northern form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jīz</i>, a northwest Germanic variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jūz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yū́</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>gij</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">ji</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">jie</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ye</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">jimme</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ihr</i>. See also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>gij</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">you</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">second-person singular subjective personal pronoun</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>Jij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>You</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weren</a>'t there.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<p><span id="attentionseekingnl" class="attentionseeking" lang="nl" title="Example sentence is for quot;jequot;, not quot;jijquot;"></span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> john (448)</h1><br></body> 
***jongen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongen</a> (264)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jonge</a></i>, the <i>-n</i> derived from declined forms. Equivalent to nominal use of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jong</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">young</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Junge</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jongens.html>jongens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A boy, any male child.
<ul><li><b>1915</b>, Nescio (pseudonum of Jan Hendrik Frederik Grönloh), <i>Titaantjes</i>, page 1.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:jongens.html>Jongens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardig.html>aardige</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jongens.html>jongens</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>Al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeg.html>zeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> 't <a href = vnd.unilang:zelf.html>zelf</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Boys</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> were — but <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> were nice <b>boys</b>. If I say so myself.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> Members of a male 'peers' group, e.g. a military unit.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> used in the plural<span class="ib-comma">,</span> used in the vocative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Informal term used to address multiple children of masculine or mixed gender;</span> kids, guys <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">may be considered insufficiently gender-inclusive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> used in the vocative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Colloquial term used by men to address other familiar men</span>; mate, dude, bro.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">familiar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A male servant, especially but not exclusively a younger one <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">using it for older men may be dated and offensive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">familiar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A male trainee or newcomer in a job.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The diminutive loses the <i>-n</i>.
</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To give birth, to have offspring, i.e. to deliver one or more young</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To multiply, grow</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord_2"><i>Zelfstandig naamwoord</i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">juust</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">juste</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">iūstus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="itc-pro">*jowestos</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂yew-</i>. <dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> ongeluk <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebeuren.html>gebeuren</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>just</b> coming back from work, when I saw an accident happen.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<li>exactly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>Zo</a>’n laffe uitvlucht <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Such a lame excuse from your part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>exactly</b> what I didn’t want to hear.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

***kamer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a> (371)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cāmere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">room, barn, house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kamara</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">camera</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">room, vault</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">καμάρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kamára</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vaulted chamber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A room, a chamber.
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with the user or owner specified</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> A bedroom.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">slaapkamer</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> with the definite article, often not specified</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A living room.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">huiskamer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">living</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">woonkamer</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with the definite article</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A special, more luxurious living room (formerly) reserved for use on Sundays and holidays, found in old houses that were inhabited by relatively affluent people.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bestekamer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">pronkkamer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">zondagskamer</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li>A chamber of a gun.</li>
<li>A chamber of parliament <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">legislative body</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A non-campus residence for students.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kot</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">studentenkamer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">studentenkot</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">canse</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norman" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norman">Old Northern French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cance</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*cadentia</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cadō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, referring to the falling of dice.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">chance</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chance</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kant.html>kant</a> (340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cant</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norman" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norman">Old Northern French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cant</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>side, face <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of an object</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deur.html>deur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kant.html>kant</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> gebouw.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> on this <b>side</b> of the building.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a> (170)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kere</i>, ultimately a derivative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn around, revolve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Kehr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time, turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kehr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">turn, direction</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ċierr</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"turn, time, occasion"; gt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chore</i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>time <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">occasion, instance</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">maal</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>reversion, reversal</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The singular form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> normally used after numerals. Thus: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>vele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keren</a></i> – many times; but: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a></i> – three times (lit. three-time).
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kiken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kīkan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kīkaną</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> (317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kint</i>, from <span </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">kinders</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kindje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">kindertje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">kindeken</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">kindelijn</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>child, kid, non-adult human
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Lieve <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mis.html>missen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jullie.html>jullie</a>. <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">typical paedagogical window message during COVID-19 measures</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Dear <b>children</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> miss you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>descendant, still a minor or irrespective of age
<dl><dd><i>In sommige patriarchale tradities <a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>blijven</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a></b> levenslang onvoorwaardelijk onderworpen <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> vaderlijk gezag, <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> aanvankelijk in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oude.html>Oude</a> Rome, in <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:houdt.html>houdt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigen.html>eigen</a> gezin <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> stichten</i>
<dl><dd>In certain patriarchal traditions, children remain subject to unconditional paternal authority for life, as originally in Ancient Rome, in other ones a son ceases to be a child by founding his own family</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">afstammeling</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">telg</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> product of influence, breeding etc.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The normal plural <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a></i>. The form <i>kinders</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> heard colloquially.</li>
<li>In compounds, the word can take the form <i>kinder-</i> or <i>kind-</i>. The former <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used more often, however.</li>
<li>The dimunitive <i>kindelijn</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now archaic, but can still be found in some fossilized songs and religious texts.</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clâer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bright, shining, ready, finished</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clārus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bright</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klaar.html>klaar</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klaar.html>klaarder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">klaarst</b>)

<ol><li>ready

<li>clear
<ul><li><b>1968</b>, Willem Johan <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> der Molen amp; Jan Wit, "Evenals <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> moede hinde" (psalm 42).
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">Evenals <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> moede hinde / <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:klaar.html>klare</a></b> water smacht, / schreeuwt <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> ziel <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> ademloos verwacht.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cōmen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">cuman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kwemaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷem-</i>.
</p>

***kop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a> (430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cop</i>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cuppa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>koppen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cup (for drinking)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>Nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kopje</a></b> thee?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">(Do you want) another <b>cup</b> of tea?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">mok</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tas</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">for animals<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial and derogatory  for humans</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> head
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Buldogs <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> angstaanjagende <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Bulldogs have a scary <b>head</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hou.html>Hou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Shut your hole!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A (male) human.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> kwaaie <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What an angry <b>guy</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>head of a nail, pin etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> slaat <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> spijker <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You hit the nail on the <b>head</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>front, lead, e.g. in a race; charge, control.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> underdog <a href = vnd.unilang:ligt.html>ligt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The underdog <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in the <b>lead</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>heading <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a text</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, headline</li>
<li>heads <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">side of a coin</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kruis</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">munt</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>pegbox (part of a stringed instrument that holds the tuning pegs)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> considered impolite to refer to someone's head with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></i>. That word normally only refers to the head of animals, although for horses, which are considered noble animals, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally used.
</p>
