***krijgen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>krijgen</a> (234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crigen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*crīgan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*krīganą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>krijgen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to receive, to come into possession of (anything ranging from concrete to abstract inputs such as news, gift, punishment, et cetera)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:familie.html>familie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> huwelijkskado <b><a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>gekregen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <b>received</b> a wedding gift from her family.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>idee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>gekregen</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klopt.html>klopt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I don't know where he <b>got</b> that idea from, but it's absolutely false.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bekomen</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to be presented with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:proberen.html>geprobeerd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> televisie <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> sluiten, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:krijg.html>krijg</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:alleen.html>alleen</a> sneeuw.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I tried to connect up my television, but I only <b>get</b> static.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to (manage to) cause to become
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:krijg.html>krijg</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> gestart!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I can't <b>get</b> my car started!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form a passive sentence with a ditransitive verb, with the original indirect object becoming the subject of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>krijgen</a></i>.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>kreeg</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> prijs uitgereikt.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a></b> given a prize.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch (a disease), to become ill with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> verkoudheid <b><a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>gekregen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I've <b>caught</b> a cold.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:krijg.html>Krijg</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> tering!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Literally "Catch tuberculosis", but more similar in force to "fuck you".</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***kun.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>kun</a> (268)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>kun</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">second-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a></i></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>Kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Can you do something for <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>As <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usual in Dutch, the <i>-t</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> dropped when the pronoun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></i> / <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></i> immediately follows the verb. However, unlike for all other verbs, the form that results <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not identical to the first-person singular, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></i>. The form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also frequently used, by analogy with regular verbs, but it may be considered nonstandard by some.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></span></li></ul>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i>Werkwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>kun</a></b>
</p>

<ol><li>(<i>in inversie</i>) tweede persoon enkelvoud tegenwoordige <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> jij-vorm <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>Kun</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klopt.html>klopt</a>?</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***kunnen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> (89)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">connen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cunnen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">cunnan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kunnaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵneh₃-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be possible

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You <b>can</b> always call <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mogen.html>mogen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> can go, to be able to go, can get
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> in!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>can</b>not <b>get</b> into my house anymore!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
